# Kachergis 2012

Kachergis et al. 2012 uncertainty- and familiarity-biased associative
model

## Usage

``` r
uncfam_sampling(X, B, C, K = 1)
```

## Arguments

- X:

  Associative weight to distribute

- B:

  Weighting of uncertainty vs. familiarity

- C:

  Decay

- K:

  Number of associations to update per word (constraint: B \<= X)

## Value

An object of class xslMod

## Examples

``` r
mod <- uncfam_sampling(X = .1, C = 1, B = .98, K = 1)
xsl_run(mod, get_example_ambiguous_condition())
#> $fits
#> $fits[[1]]
#> $fits[[1]]$sims
#> $fits[[1]]$sims[[1]]
#> $perf
#>         1         2         3         4 
#> 0.6666667 0.1111111 0.1111111 0.1111111 
#>

#>      1    2    3    4
```
